About the Role

We are seeking a proactive and detail-oriented Pre-Sales Business Analyst to play a key role in supporting the sales cycle by translating customer needs into clear, solution-ready requirements and documentation. The role involves close collaboration with the PMO Delivery Director (primary reporting), as well as providing pre-sales support to the Strategic Business Director and Sales & Customer Success Executive through requirement gathering, solution scoping, and preparation of technical inputs for proposals and demos. The ideal candidate will ensure customer expectations are accurately understood, documented, and aligned with product capabilities before transition to delivery teams, and may also support early delivery phases to ensure smooth implementation planning.

Key Responsibilities:

  1. Pre-Sales Discovery & Requirements Gathering

    • Attend client discovery calls and demos alongside the Strategic Business Director or Sales & Customer Success Executive.
    • Capture and document business needs, workflows, and functional expectations.
    • Clarify objectives, use cases, and customer challenges early in the sales cycle.
    • Translate discussions into structured requirement notes or actionable briefs.

  2. Solution Scoping & Technical Documentation

    • Develop preliminary solution outlines, scope summaries, and feature mappings.
    • Create draft Business Requirement Documents (BRDs) or Functional Specifications (FSDs) when required.
    • Produce workflow diagrams, wireframes, or configuration concepts with support from the designer team when needed (e.g., using Figma, Lucidchart, Visio).
    • Align proposed solutions with product capabilities and delivery feasibility in coordination with PMO.

  3. Proposal & Technical Input Support

    • Contribute the technical and functional sections of proposals, SOWs, capability decks, and solution documentation.
    • Provide supporting material such as feature breakdowns, workflow references, screenshots, or demo visuals.
    • Coordinate with PMs, Product Teams, and Solutions Architects to validate effort, timelines, and scope.
    • Ensure documentation libraries, templates, and proposal-related assets remain current and accurate.

  4. Demo Support & Client Workshops

    • Assist in tailoring and preparing demos based on client requirements.
    • Support solution walkthroughs by demonstrating functionality, workflows, or configuration concepts.
    • Capture questions, required modifications, and follow-up actions from demos or workshops.
    • Provide functional clarity to the Sales & Customer Success Executive and Product Delivery teams.

  5. Collaboration with Sales, Marketing & Technical Teams

    • Work with the Sales & Customer Success Executive to align scope, requirements, and customer expectations.
    • Provide technical input to marketing collateral when showcasing system workflows or configurations.
    • Support design and content teams with diagrams, Figma links, functionality clarifications, or feature visuals.
    • Coordinate early solution feasibility with PMO, developers, and product architects.

  6. Delivery Handover & Flexible BA Support (Post-Sale)

    • Prepare structured handover notes for PMO, BA, and delivery teams to begin implementation.
    • Clarify assumptions, workflows, deliverables, and effort during pre-kick-off activities.
    • Where needed, transition temporarily into a Business Analyst role during project initiation.
    • Support configuration workshops, requirement validation, and solution alignment during onboarding.

Preferred Skills, Experience & Background:

  • Experience: 2–4 years in pre-sales, business analysis, solution consulting, or functional coordination in a software/SaaS/IT environment.
  • Experience working with delivery, product, or technical teams to translate requirements into solutions.
  • Familiarity with software implementation lifecycles and client discovery processes.

Tools & Systems:

  • Strong experience with Microsoft Office/365 (Excel, PowerPoint, Word).
  • Working knowledge of Jira or similar project/issue tracking tools.
  • Experience using diagramming or workflow tools (e.g., Visio, Lucidchart, Figma, Miro).

Skills & Capabilities:

  • Excellent written and verbal communication skills.
  • Ability to gather, structure, and document requirements clearly.
  • Strong analytical and problem-solving abilities.
  • Ability to collaborate with cross-functional teams (Sales, PMO, Delivery).
  • Good attention to detail and ability to handle multiple priorities.

Education:

  • Bachelor’s degree in IT, Business, Engineering, Computer Science, or related field.

Preferred:

  • Industry & Product Knowledge: Exposure to Lean, manufacturing, logistics, or process improvement environments. Understanding of SaaS platforms, workflow-based systems, or ERP/MES/QMS tools.
  • Proposal & Demo Involvement: Experience contributing to proposals, solution decks, or SOWs. Exposure to software demos, configuration showcases, or pre-sales workshops.
  • Collaboration & Market Alignment: Experience working with UK/Europe or international clients. Ability to provide input into marketing or sales collateral (from a functional perspective).
  • Tools & Technology (Nice-to-Haves): Familiarity with HubSpot or CRM platforms (viewing/updating deal notes, not ownership). Experience using Figma or similar design reference tools (for workflows/UI mapping). Awareness of AI tools (ChatGPT, Copilot, Jasper, etc.) for documentation support.

The ideal candidate has deep expertise in enterprise commerce systems, cloud architecture, and system integrations. You will guide development teams, ensure best practices in solution design, and ultimately take full ownership of the architecture and development transition from the vendor.

Responsibilities:

Architecture & Design

  • Define the end-to-end migration architecture from SAP B2B to Optimizely, including CMS, Commerce, and PIM integration.
  • Design scalable, secure, and high-performance frameworks aligned with business goals.
  • Establish data migration strategies for products, pricing, and customer hierarchies.
  • Ensure API integration between SAP, Optimizely, and other enterprise systems.

Technical Leadership

  • Lead and mentor development teams on best practices and coding standards.
  • Collaborate with Optimizely consultants and internal teams to validate feasibility and technical approach.
  • Drive DevOps strategy for CI/CD pipelines, containerization, and cloud deployment.

Project Ownership

  • Act as the technical owner of the migration project, taking over from vendor after initial phases.
  • Ensure alignment with enterprise security and compliance standards.
  • Provide technical guidance during feasibility analysis and pilot module migration.

Collaboration & Communication

  • Work closely with Business Analysts to translate requirements into technical solutions.
  • Communicate architecture decisions to stakeholders and leadership in business-friendly terms.
  • Support QA teams with test strategy for performance, integration, and security.

Preferred Skills

  • SAP B2B Architecture: Deep understanding of SAP Commerce Cloud, Back Office, and integration patterns.
  • B2B Platform: Hands-on experience with CMS and Commerce Cloud platforms, specifically Optimizely.
  • Optimizely PIM & Spire: Strong knowledge of Optimizely Product Information Management (PIM) and Spire framework for modern commerce experiences.
  • .NET Development: Proficient in .NET Core and ASP.NET, essential for Optimizely development.
  • Cloud Architecture: Strong knowledge of Azure PaaS, commonly used for hosting Optimizely solutions.
  • Azure Active Directory: Experience with identity and access management using Azure AD.
  • API Design & Integration: Skilled in RESTful services, SAP APIs, and Optimizely endpoints.
